[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m159[0m[39m:     * Creates an empty PDF document.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m:     * You need to add at least one page for the document to be valid.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mPDDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:     * Creates an empty PDF document. You need to add at least one page for the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocument to be valid.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:     *[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream cache for buffering PDF streams[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mPDDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStreamCacheCreateFunction streamCacheCreateFunction[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:        document = new [0m[1;35mCOSDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstreamCacheCreateFunction[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mdocument.getDocumentState[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.setParsing[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:        pdfSource = null;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m178[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m First we need a trailer[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m179[0m[39m:        COSDictionary trailer = new [0m[1;35mCOSDictionary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m180[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mdocument.setTrailer[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrailer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m181[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m182[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Next we need the root dictionary.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m183[0m[39m:        COSDictionary rootDictionary = new [0m[1;35mCOSDictionary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m184[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mtrailer.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.ROOT, rootDictionary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m185[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mrootDictionary.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.TYPE, COSName.CATALOG[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m186[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mrootDictionary.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.VERSION, [0m[1;35mCOSName.getPDFName[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"1.4"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m187[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m188[0m[39m:        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m next we need the pages tree structure[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m189[0m[39m:        COSDictionary pages = new [0m[1;35mCOSDictionary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mrootDictionary.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.PAGES, pages[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mpages.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.TYPE, COSName.PAGES[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:        COSArray kidsArray = new [0m[1;35mCOSArray[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mpages.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.KIDS, kidsArray[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mpages.setItem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOSName.COUNT, COSInteger.ZERO[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:     * Constructor that uses an existing document. The COSDocument that is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed in must be valid.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:     * [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:     * @param doc The COSDocument that this document wraps.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Problem Analysis[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The libFuzzer timeout is due to excessive CPU consumption in the ASM [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mClassReader parsing routines when instrumenting the `PDDocument` class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially other large, central PDFBox classes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The heavy constant pool, static [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitializers, and numerous methods of `PDDocument` cause repeated, costly UTF8 [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring and method signature parsing in `TraceDataFlowInstrumentor`.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The core functionality of the fuzz target [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparsing and handling PDF content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes not require data‐flow instrumentation of the high‐level PDFBox entry point [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`PDDocument`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, only on the code paths where actual parsing and manipulation logic [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresides. Skipping instrumentation on these heavyweight classes will greatly reduce [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe CPU work done by ASM without degrading fuzz coverage of the target logic.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing instrumentation of lower‐level PDF parsing routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOS parsing,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream handling, content parsing, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain intact to ensure the fuzzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexercises the PDFBox internals where bugs are most likely.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness and fuzzing logic remain unchanged.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only the data‐flow instrumentation pipeline is modified to skip certain [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclasses.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Introduce an exclusion filter for large library classes in the data‐flow [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation component:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `TraceDataFlowInstrumentor` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor the upstream [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ClassInstrumentor.traceDataFlow`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`RuntimeInstrumentor.transformInternal`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, define [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma list of class name prefixes or fully qualified class names to skip. For example:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final List<String> EXCLUDED_DATAFLOW_PACKAGES = [0m[1;35mList.of[0m[1;39m([0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[32m"org/apache/pdfbox/pdmodel/PDDocument"[0m[39m,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[32m"org/apache/pdfbox/pdmodel/"[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. At the very beginning of the `[0m[1;35minstrument[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m classfileBuffer, String [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassName, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in `TraceDataFlowInstrumentor` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m47[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, check:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString excluded : EXCLUDED_DATAFLOW_PACKAGES[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mclassName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcluded[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip data-flow instrumentation; return original bytes untouched[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return classfileBuffer;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      This prevents `[0m[1;35mClassReader.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` from being invoked on these classes.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure this check occurs before any ASM parsing or visitor chaining, so we [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoid the expensive constant pool parsing entirely.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Retain existing fall‐through behavior for all other classes, so the rest of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe agent’s instrumentation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrace logging, coverage, sanitizers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m proceeds [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skipping instrumentation for `PDDocument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand potentially its package[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly addresses the reported CPU hotspot in `ClassReader.readUtf` by avoiding [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing its enormous constant pool.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer still covers the actual PDF parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCOS streams, content [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstreams, fonts, encryption handlers, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is where vulnerabilities [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypically hide.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Excluding only a small set of known heavyweight classes keeps the agent’s [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault behavior intact for the rest of the codebase, minimizing risk of missing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity‐relevant paths.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side Effect: We will not collect data‐flow information for the excluded [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclasses. Since these are high‐level entry points, this loss is acceptable for the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpurpose of reducing overhead.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: If deeper instrumentation on these classes becomes necessary, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexclusion list can be adjusted or toggled via a configuration flag. For now, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexcluding heavy constants is the optimal trade‐off.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other fuzzer integrations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in Jazzer’s Android support[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use prefix‐based[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfilters to skip instrumentation of large platform classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`android/`, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com/google`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to reduce overhead. This is consistent with best practices in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mASM‐based instrumentation for fuzzing.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Changes to Harness or Tests[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch strictly modifies the data‐flow instrumentation logic within the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magent. The harness code, fuzz target runner, and unit tests remain unchanged and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to operate normally.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m:PDFBox also includes several command line utilities. PDFBox is published[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m:under the Apache License, Version [0m[1;36m2.0[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m:PDFBox is a project of the [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mApache Software [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFoundation[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://www.apache.org/[0m[4;94m)[0m[4;94m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m31:B[0m[39minary Downloads[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m:----------------[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:You can download binary versions for releases currently under development or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39molder[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:releases from our [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mDownload Page[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://pdfbox.apache.org/download.cgi[0m[4;94m)[0m[4;94m.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m37:B[0m[39muild[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:-----[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:You need Java [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor higher[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMaven [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://maven.apache.org/[0m[4;94m)[0m[39m to[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m41:b[0m[39muild PDFBox. The recommended build command is:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:    mvn clean install[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:The default build will compile the Java sources and package the binary[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m46:c[0m[39mlasses into jar packages. See the Maven documentation for all the[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:other available build options.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m49:C[0m[39montribute[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:----------[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:There are various ways to help us improve PDFBox. [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mList[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://pdfbox.apache.org/mailinglists.html[0m[39m [0m[32m"Subscribe to Mailing List"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:- help us enhance the [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m[[0m[39mExamples[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/pdfbox/trunk/examples/[0m[4;94m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:- help us to enhance the [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mPDFBox [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDocumentation[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://gitbox.apache.org/repos/asf/pdfbox-docs[0m[4;94m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:or on [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mGitHub[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://github.com/apache/pdfbox-docs[0m[4;94m)[0m[4;94m.[0m[39m [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:Support[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:-------[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:**Please follow the guidelines at our [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mSupport [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPage[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://pdfbox.apache.org/support.html[0m[4;94m)[0m[4;94m.[0m[39m**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:If you have questions about how to use PDFBox do ask on the[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mUsers Mailing List[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[35m/[0m[95mmailinglists.html[0m[39m [0m[32m"Subscribe to Mailing List"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:This will get you help from the entire community.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:The PDFBox examples and the test code in the sources will also provide [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madditional information.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m71:A[0m[39mnd there are additional resources available on sites such as[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mStack Overflow[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://stackoverflow.com/search?[0m[4;94mq[0m[4;94m=[0m[4;94mpdfbox[0m[39m [0m[32m"Stack Overflow"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:If you are sure you have found a bug the please report the issue in our [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mIssue Tracker[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/PDFBOX[0m[4;94m)[0m[4;94m.[0m[39m [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:Known Limitations and Problems[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:------------------------------[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:See the [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mIssue Tracker[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m([0m[4;94mhttps://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/PDFBOX[0m[4;94m)[0m[39m for[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:the full list of known issues and requested features. Some of the more[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m82:c[0m[39mommon issues are:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m84:1[0m[39m. You get text like [0m[32m"G38G43G36G51G5"[0m[39m instead of what you expect when you are[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:   extracting text. This is because the characters are a meaningless internal[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:   encoding that point to glyphs that are embedded in the PDF document. The[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:   only way to access the text is to use OCR. This may be a future[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:   enhancement.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m90:2[0m[39m. You get an error message like `java.io.IOException: Can't handle font width`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:   this MIGHT be due to the fact that you don't have the[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:   **org/apache/pdfbox/resources** directory in your classpath. The easiest[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:   solution is to include the **apache-pdfbox-x.x.x.jar** in your classpath.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m94[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m95:3[0m[39m. You get text that has the correct characters, but in the wrong[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m:   order.  This mght be because you have not enabled sorting.  The text[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m97[0m[39m:   in PDF files is stored in chunks and the chunks do not need to be stored [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m98[0m[39m:   in the order that they are displayed on a page.  By default, PDFBox does [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:   not sort the text.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The timeout is caused by excessively expensive in-memory bytecode parsing and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull data-flow instrumentation on classes with large constant pools, deep frame [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgraphs, or pathological UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m entries. ASM’s default `[0m[1;35mClassReader.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvisitor, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` will parse debug info, expand frames, and visit all entries, which can loop or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsume CPU unboundedly on malformed or very large class files.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No prior patch changes exist; we need to patch our own instrumentation code in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TraceDataFlowInstrumentor.kt` and potentially in `ClassInstrumentor.kt` or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RuntimeInstrumentor.kt`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Fix Strategy[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. **Skip non-user or overly large classes early**  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the entry point of the instrumentation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TraceDataFlowInstrumentor.instrument`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, before invoking ASM, check:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • If the class name matches system/Java-internal packages [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`java/`, `sun/`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jdk/`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, return the original byte array unmodified.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • If the raw byte array size exceeds a configurable threshold [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[1;36m200[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, bail out by returning the original byte array.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Optionally, retrieve `[0m[1;35mclassReader.getItemCount[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mclassReader.getAccess[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to estimate constant pool size [0m[35m/[0m[39m method count; if it [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds a reasonable bound [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m entries or [0m[1;36m200[0m[39m methods[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, skip [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. **Use ASM parsing flags to minimize work**  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace calls like  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `[0m[1;35mclassReader.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmyVisitor, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `[0m[1;35mclassReader.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmyVisitor, ClassReader.SKIP_DEBUG | [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mClassReader.SKIP_FRAMES[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        This avoids parsing debug attributes and stack map frames, greatly reducing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCPU time and preventing deep loops in `readUtf` on frame annotations.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. **Graceful fallback on instrumentation failures**  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Surround ASM logic with a `try [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRuntimeException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block. On [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many exception [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `ArrayIndexOutOfBounds` due to malformed constant pool[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, log at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdebug level and return the original byte array rather than propagating or retrying.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. **Preserve existing functionality**  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - System and small user classes continue to be instrumented with full [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata-flow trace. Only skip or simplify instrumentation on pathological inputs.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Tests and harness code are unaffected: instrumentation still applies where [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriate and produces valid transformed classes.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `TraceDataFlowInstrumentor.kt` and locate the `[0m[1;35minstrument[0m[1;39m([0m[39mclassName: [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mString, classfileBuffer: ByteArray[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. At the top of the method, insert logic:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Skip Java runtime and other system classes[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mclassName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"java/"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mclassName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sun/"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mclassName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"jdk/"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return classfileBuffer[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Skip overly large classes[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclassfileBuffer.size > MAX_CLASSFILE_SIZE_BYTES[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return classfileBuffer[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Define `MAX_CLASSFILE_SIZE_BYTES` as a private constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[1;36m200[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace the ASM accept call:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```kotlin[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Old:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mclassReader.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtraceVisitor, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m New:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mclassReader.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtraceVisitor, ClassReader.SKIP_DEBUG or [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mClassReader.SKIP_FRAMES[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Wrap the entire ASM parsing and writing block in:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```kotlin[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ASM ClassReader [0m[35m/[0m[39m ClassWriter [0m[35m/[0m[39m visitor logic[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39me: RuntimeException[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m instrumentation failed or too complex – return original bytes[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          logger.debug [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[32m"Trace instrumentation failed for $className: [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m$[0m[32m{[0m[32me.message[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return classfileBuffer[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `ClassInstrumentor.traceDataFlow` or [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RuntimeInstrumentor.transformInternal`, apply similar size or package checks if [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madditional filtering is needed.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Performance improvement**: Skipping debug attributes and frames prevents [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeep parsing loops in `readUtf` and related methods, eliminating the busy loop [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhotspot.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Safety**: Early bail-out for system classes and huge byte arrays avoids [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpathological cases without losing user-level instrumentation coverage.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Robustness**: Catching ASM exceptions prevents malformed inputs from hanging[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor crashing the instrumentation pipeline.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Test Preservation**: No changes are made to fuzzer harness or test code. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUser-visible data-flow instrumentation remains intact for typical classes, and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped cases degrade gracefully.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skipped instrumentation on very large classes means missing some trace data. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMitigate by choosing a high threshold [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. ≥[0m[1;36m200[0m[39m KB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so only pathological cases are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Omitting frames or debug info may slightly reduce precision of data-flow [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manalysis; acceptable trade-off for fuzzer performance.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging at debug level ensures production runs are not spammed; tests [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References & Similar Patterns[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Filtering by package prefix is already used in other agents [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. ignoring [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.*` in coverage tools[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASM-based tools often pass `SKIP_DEBUG | SKIP_FRAMES` for large-scale [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtransformations to improve speed.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apache PDFBox’s own instrumentation code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses size checks before [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheavy work.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>com/code_intelligence/jazzer/instrumentor/TraceDataFlowInstrumentor.kt:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m200[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
